This is currently called from the 'main' thread, which also\n137: // handles 'push' requests and close - the code will eventually call the 'push' code, and it needs more mutex\n138: // protection. Original code avoided the mutexes by doing both 'push' and 'process requests' in same thread.\n139: func (s *DiscoveryServer) processRequest(req *discovery.DiscoveryRequest, con *Connection) error {\n140: \tstype := v3.GetShortType(req.TypeUrl)\n141: \tlog.Debugf(\"ADS:%s: REQ %s resources:%d nonce:%s version:%s \", stype,\n142: \t\tcon.ID(), len(req.ResourceNames), req.ResponseNonce, req.VersionInfo)\n143: \tif req.TypeUrl == v3.HealthInfoType {\n144: \t\ts.handleWorkloadHealthcheck(con.proxy, req)\n145: \t\treturn nil\n146: \t}\n147: \n148: \t// For now, don't let xDS piggyback debug requests start watchers.\n149: \tif strings.HasPrefix(req.TypeUrl, v3.DebugType) {\n150: \t\treturn s.pushXds(con,\n151: \t\t\t&model.WatchedResource{TypeUrl: req.TypeUrl, ResourceNames: sets.New(req.ResourceNames...)},\n152: \t\t\t&model.PushRequest{Full: true, Push: con.proxy.LastPushContext, Forced: true})\n153: \t}\n154: \n155: \tshouldRespond, delta := xds.ShouldRespond(con.proxy, con.ID(), req)\n156: \tif !shouldRespond {\n157: \t\treturn nil\n158: \t}\n159: \n160: \trequest := &model.PushRequest{\n161: \t\tFull:   true,\n162: \t\tPush:   con.proxy.LastPushContext,\n163: \t\tReason: model.NewReasonStats(model.ProxyRequest),\n164: \n165: \t\t// The usage of LastPushTime (rather than time.Now()), is critical here for correctness; This time\n166: \t\t// is used by the XDS cache to determine if a entry is stale. If we use Now() with an old push context,\n167: \t\t// we may end up overriding active cache entries with stale ones.\n168: \t\tStart:  con.proxy.LastPushTime,\n169: \t\tDelta:  delta,\n170: \t\tForced: true,\n171: \t}\n172: \n173: \t// SidecarScope for the proxy may not have been updated based on this pushContext.\n174: \t// It can happen when `processRequest` comes after push context has been updated(s.initPushContext),\n175: \t// but proxy's SidecarScope has been updated(s.computeProxyState -> SetSidecarScope) due to optimizations that skip sidecar scope\n176: \t// computation.\n177: \tif con.proxy.SidecarScope != nil && con.proxy.SidecarScope.Version != request.Push.PushVersion {\n178: \t\ts.computeProxyState(con.proxy, request)\n179: \t}\n180: \treturn s.pushXds(con, con.proxy.GetWatchedResource(req.TypeUrl), request)\n181: }\n182: \n183: // StreamAggregatedResources implements the ADS interface.\n184: func (s *DiscoveryServer) StreamAggregatedResources(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n185: \treturn s.Stream(stream)\n186: }\n187: \n188: func (s *DiscoveryServer) Stream(stream DiscoveryStream) error {\n189: \tif knativeEnv != \"\" && firstRequest.Load() {\n190: \t\t// How scaling works in knative is the first request is the \"loading\" request. During\n191: \t\t// loading request, concurrency=1. Once that request is done, concurrency is enabled.\n192: \t\t// However, the XDS stream is long lived, so the first request would block all others. As a\n193: \t\t// result, we should exit the first request immediately; clients will retry.\n194: \t\tfirstRequest.Store(false)\n195: \t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server warmup not complete; try again\")\n196: \t}\n197: \t// Check if server is ready to accept clients and process new requests.\n198: \t// Currently ready means caches have been synced and hence can build\n199: \t// clusters correctly. Without this check, InitContext() call below would\n200: \t// initialize with empty config, leading to reconnected Envoys losing\n201: \t// configuration. This is an additional safety check inaddition to adding\n202: \t// cachesSynced logic to readiness probe to handle cases where kube-proxy\n203: \t// ip tables update latencies.\n204: \t// See https://github.com/istio/istio/issues/25495.\n205: \tif !s.IsServerReady() {\n206: \t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unavailable, \"server is not ready to serve discovery information\")\n207: \t}\n208: \n209: \tctx := stream.Context()\n210: \tpeerAddr := \"0.0.0.0\"\n211: \tif peerInfo, ok := peer.FromContext(ctx); ok {\n212: \t\tpeerAddr = peerInfo.Addr.String()\n213: \t}\n214: \n215: \tif err := s.WaitForRequestLimit(stream.Context()); err != nil {\n216: \t\tlog.Warnf(\"ADS: %q exceeded rate limit: %v\", peerAddr, err)\n217: \t\treturn status.Errorf(codes.ResourceExhausted, \"request rate limit exceeded: %v\", err)\n218: \t}\n219: \n220: \tids, err := s.authenticate(ctx)\n221: \tif err != nil {\n222: \t\treturn status.Error(codes.Unauthenticated, err.Error())\n223: \t}\n224: \tif ids != nil {\n225: \t\tlog.Debugf(\"Authenticated XDS: %v with identity %v\", peerAddr, ids)\n226: \t} else {\n227: \t\tlog.Debugf(\"Unauthenticated XDS: %s\", peerAddr)\n228: \t}\n229: \n230: \t// InitContext returns immediately if the context was already initialized.\n231: \ts.globalPushContext().InitContext(s.Env, nil, nil)\n232: \tcon := newConnection(peerAddr, stream)\n233: \tcon.ids = ids\n234: \tcon.s = s\n235: \treturn xds.Stream(con)\n236: }\n237: \n238: // update the node associated with the connection, after receiving a packet from envoy, also adds the connection\n239: // to the tracking map.\n240: func (s *DiscoveryServer) initConnection(node *core.Node, con *Connection, identities []string) error {\n241: \t// Setup the initial proxy metadata\n242: \tproxy, err := s.initProxyMetadata(node)\n243: \tif err != nil {\n244: \t\treturn err\n245: \t}\n246: \t// Check if proxy cluster has an alias configured, if yes use that as cluster ID for this proxy.\n247: \tif alias, exists := s.ClusterAliases[proxy.Metadata.ClusterID]; []*IstioEndpoint)\\n312: \\n313: // XDSUpdater is used for direct updates of the xDS model and incremental push.\\n314: // Pilot uses multiple registries - for example each K8S cluster is a registry\\n315: // instance. Each registry is responsible for tracking a set\\n316: // of endpoints associated with mesh services, and calling the EDSUpdate on changes.\\n317: // A registry may group endpoints for a service in smaller subsets - for example by\\n318: // deployment, or to deal with very large number of endpoints for a service. We want\\n319: // to avoid passing around large objects - like full list of endpoints for a registry,\\n320: // or the full list of endpoints for a service across registries, since it limits\\n321: // scalability.\\n322: //\\n323: // Future optimizations will include grouping the endpoints by labels, gateway or region to\\n324: // reduce the time when subsetting or split-horizon is used. This design assumes pilot\\n325: // tracks all endpoints in the mesh and they fit in RAM - so limit is few M endpoints.\\n326: // It is possible to split the endpoint tracking in future.\\n327: type XDSUpdater interface {\\n328: \\t// EDSUpdate is called when the list of endpoints or labels in a Service is changed.\\n329: \\t// For each cluster and hostname, the full list of active endpoints (including empty list)\\n330: \\t// must be sent. {"type":"assistant","message":{"model":"claude-haiku-4-5-20251001","id":"msg_012hnR44NioxPzGS7RxHHvQn","type":"message","role":"assistant","content":[{"type":"tool_use","id":"toolu_01Njd8KxiLzuN3H2r4DeDRNr","name":"Write","input":{"file_path":"/workspace/documentation.md","content":"# Istio Pilot Discovery Service Architecture\n\n## Overview\n\nPilot's Discovery Service is the core subsystem responsible for serving Envoy Proxy instances with dynamic service mesh configuration via the xDS (Envoy Discovery Service) APIs. The Discovery Service translates high-level Istio resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Gateways, etc.) into low-level Envoy-specific resource configurations (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) and maintains real-time synchronization as the service mesh state evolves.\n\nThe architecture follows a **push-based model** where Pilot proactively delivers configuration updates to proxies rather than waiting for proxies to poll. It supports Envoy's xDS v3 protocol in both state-of-the-world (full) and incremental push modes, with sophisticated debouncing and rate-limiting to handle high-frequency updates efficiently in large-scale meshes.\n\n---\n\n## Component 1: DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**File**: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is the central gRPC server component that:\n- Implements Envoy's xDS APIs (ADS, CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS)\n- Manages active proxy connections via the `adsClients` map\n- Coordinates configuration pushes with debouncing and rate limiting\n- Maintains the global configuration snapshot (PushContext)\n- Serves as the interface between Istio's configuration model and Envoy proxies\n\n### Structure\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env *model.Environment                           // Pilot's data model\n    Generators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Per-type resource generators\n    adsClients map[string]*Connection                // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex                     // Protects adsClients\n\n    pushChannel chan *model.PushRequest              // Debounce buffer\n    pushQueue *PushQueue                             // Queue before actual push\n\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}                // Semaphore for concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter                   // Throttle incoming requests\n\n    Cache model.XdsCache                             // XDS resource cache\n    DebounceOptions DebounceOptions                  // Debounce timing config\n}\n```\n\n### Key Methods\n\n#### 1. **StreamAggregatedResources / Stream()**\nImplements the gRPC service method that establishes a bidirectional stream with an Envoy proxy.\n\n```\nConnection Flow:\n  1. Proxy connects → gRPC calls Stream()\n  2. Stream() checks server readiness and applies rate limiting\n  3. Authenticates the connection (mutual TLS verification)\n  4. Creates a Connection wrapper for the stream\n  5. Hands off to xds.Stream() for managing the connection lifecycle\n```\n\nThe server waits for `CachesSynced()` before accepting connections, ensuring proxies don't receive incomplete configuration during startup.\n\n#### 2. **ConfigUpdate(req \\*PushRequest)**\nCalled by event handlers (config watchers, service registry updates) to request a configuration push.\n\n```\nFlow:\n  1. Receives push request with updated configs/services\n  2. Sends to pushChannel for debouncing\n  3. handleUpdates() debouncer merges multiple rapid requests\n  4. Eventually calls Push() once config settles\n```\n\n#### 3. **Push(req \\*PushRequest)**\nExecutes the actual push once debouncing is complete.\n\n```\nFor Full Pushes:\n  1. Creates new PushContext by calling initPushContext()\n    - Rebuilds service index from service registry\n    - Rebuilds VirtualService and DestinationRule indexes\n    - Recomputes sidecar scopes\n    - Initializes ambient index\n  2. Calls dropCacheForRequest() to clear cached xDS responses\n  3. Calls AdsPushAll(req) to broadcast to connected proxies\n\nFor Incremental Pushes:\n  1. Reuses existing PushContext\n  2. Only clears cache for updated configs\n  3. Calls AdsPushAll() for affected proxies\n```\n\n#### 4. **AdsPushAll(req \\*PushRequest)**\nBroadcasts a push to all connected proxies.\n\n```\nAlgorithm:\n  1. Iterates through adsClients map (protected by RWMutex)\n  2. For each proxy connection, determines if push is necessary:\n     - Uses ProxyNeedsPush callback to filter proxies\n     - Checks if proxy is affected by specific config changes\n  3. Enqueues push event into pushQueue for the proxy\n  4. Returns immediately; actual push happens asynchronously in sendPushes()\n```\n\n#### 5. **sendPushes(stopCh)**\nBackground goroutine that processes the push queue.\n\n```\nFlow:\n  1. Dequeues a proxy from pushQueue\n  2. Acquires a slot from concurrentPushLimit semaphore\n  3. Calls pushConnection() to compute and send config for the proxy\n  4. Releases semaphore slot\n  5. Marks proxy as done in queue\n  6. Repeats until stopCh signals shutdown\n```\n\n### Cache Management\n\nThe DiscoveryServer maintains a typed XDS resource cache (`Cache`) that stores computed Envoy resources (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints). This cache:\n- Avoids recomputing identical resources for multiple proxies\n- Is cleared on full pushes or when specific config types change\n- Is optimized for incremental pushes where only affected resources are regenerated\n- Supports different cache backends (enabled/disabled via features)\n\n### Concurrency Control\n\n**Debouncing**: Rapid configuration changes are merged before generating Envoy resources:\n- `DebounceAfter`: Minimum quiet time to wait after last event\n- `debounceMax`: Maximum time to wait regardless of event frequency\n- Prevents configuration churn from flooding proxies\n\n**Rate Limiting**:\n- `RequestRateLimit`: Throttles new incoming XDS requests from clients\n- `concurrentPushLimit`: Limits concurrent xDS resource generation to prevent resource exhaustion\n\n---\n\n## Component 2: ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Files**: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/ads_test.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) stream handler manages the life cycle of individual proxy connections, processes discovery requests, and coordinates push delivery to single proxies.\n\n### Connection Type\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                          // Wraps gRPC stream\n    node *core.Node                         // Envoy's metadata\n    proxy *model.Proxy                      // Istio's proxy representation\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream        // For Delta xDS mode\n    s *DiscoveryServer                      // Parent server reference\n    ids []string                            // Authenticated identities\n}\n```\n\nThe `Connection` acts as a bridge between Envoy's gRPC stream and Istio's internal proxy model, translating between the two representations.\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n#### 1. **Stream Establishment**\n```\nStream() → initConnection() → newConnection() → xds.Stream()\n\nProcess:\n  1. Stream() receives gRPC connection from Envoy\n  2. Checks server readiness\n  3. Applies rate limiting to prevent thundering herd\n  4. Authenticates connection (validates mTLS identity)\n  5. Initializes PushContext if not already done\n  6. Creates Connection wrapper\n  7. Hands to xds.Stream() which manages the actual message exchange\n```\n\n#### 2. **initConnection()**\nInitializes proxy metadata when receiving the first discovery request.\n\n```go\nExecution:\n  1. Parses Envoy's node metadata (pod name, namespace, IP, etc.)\n  2. Creates Proxy object from node metadata\n  3. Applies cluster alias mapping (multi-cluster translation)\n  4. Adds connection to adsClients map with a unique ID\n  5. Sets proxy's LastPushContext for monotonic push ordering\n  6. Registers handlers for this proxy with service registry\n```\n\n#### 3. **Request Processing: processRequest()**\nHandles individual discovery requests from the proxy.\n\n```go\nProcess:\n  1. Extracts resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS)\n  2. Checks if proxy should respond based on nonce/version\n  3. Creates PushRequest with:\n     - Full=true for missing resources or debug requests\n     - Delta for resource subscription changes\n     - Forced=true to bypass recent push filters\n  4. Calls pushXds() to generate and send response\n```\n\n**Key Insight**: `processRequest()` treats a discovery request as a push trigger, allowing proxies to explicitly request resources they're interested in.\n\n#### 4. **Push Delivery: pushConnection()**\nComputes and sends configuration for a single proxy.\n\n```go\nAlgorithm (per WatchedResource type):\n  1. Looks up the appropriate generator:\n     - CdsGenerator for Clusters\n     - RdsGenerator for Routes\n     - LdsGenerator for Listeners\n     - EdsGenerator for Endpoints\n  2. Calls generator.Generate(proxy, req) to build Envoy resources\n  3. Compares new resources with cached version\n  4. Sends only resources that changed (for incremental pushes)\n  5. Wraps in DiscoveryResponse with nonce and version info\n  6. Sends via gRPC stream to proxy\n```\n\nThe generator selection is proxy-aware; different proxies can use different generators (e.g., sidecar vs. gateway).\n\n#### 5. **Connection Cleanup: closeConnection()**\nRemoves proxy from active connection map when stream closes.\n\n```\nExecution:\n  1. Removes connection from adsClients\n  2. Removes proxy from service registry watchers\n  3. Unregisters proxy-specific handlers\n```\n\n### Push Coordination Through Events\n\nPushes are delivered via the `Event` structure:\n\n```go\ntype Event struct {\n    pushRequest *model.PushRequest\n    done func()                  // Must be called to signal completion\n}\n```\n\nThe `done()` callback ensures backpressure: the push queue won't dequeue the next proxy until `done()` is called, preventing the system from being overwhelmed.\n\n---\n\n## Component 3: PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**File**: `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of mesh configuration built once per full push. It:\n- Holds pre-computed indices of services, routes, policies, and security configurations\n- Serves as the authoritative configuration source for resource generators\n- Tracks push metrics and errors per proxy\n- Enables deterministic config translation across the fleet\n\n### Structure\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service catalog\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex                        // Services indexed by namespace/visibility\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex          // VirtualServices by gateway\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex        // DestinationRules consolidated\n\n    // Security and networking\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies            // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies             // AuthorizationPolicy resources\n\n    // Configuration metadata\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex                        // Sidecar scopes per namespace\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex                        // Gateways by namespace\n\n    // Computed state\n    exportToDefaults exportToDefaults                // Default visibility rules\n    clusterLocalHosts ClusterLocalHosts              // Cluster-local service names\n\n    // Tracking\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus  // Push errors per proxy\n    PushVersion string                               // Unique push identifier\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization: InitContext()\n\nCalled once per full push to rebuild configuration.\n\n```\nExecution (createNewContext):\n  1. initServiceRegistry()\n    - Fetches all services from ServiceDiscovery (Kubernetes + ServiceEntry)\n    - Builds serviceIndex with private/public/exported-to organization\n    - Aggregates endpoints across multiple registries/clusters\n\n  2. initVirtualServices()\n    - Fetches all VirtualService resources\n    - Indexes by namespace, gateway, and delegation\n    - Validates references to services and subsets\n\n  3. initDestinationRules()\n    - Fetches all DestinationRule resources\n    - Consolidates rules for the same service across namespaces\n    - Pre-computes subset information\n\n  4. initAuthnPolicies() / initAuthorizationPolicies()\n    - Fetches authentication and authorization policies\n    - Builds efficient lookup structures by namespace/service\n\n  5. initSidecarScopes() [last, as it depends on all above]\n    - Computes SidecarScope for each namespace\n    - Default SidecarScope if none defined\n    - Determines ingress/egress visibility for workloads\n\n  6. initGateways() / initAmbient() / initWasmPlugins() / etc.\n    - Pre-computed data for gateways, ambient mesh, WASM plugins\n```\n\n**Incremental Updates**: If a previous PushContext exists and only specific config types changed, `updateContext()` reuses unchanged indices:\n\n```\nLogic:\n  if ServiceEntry changed → rebuild ServiceIndex else copy from previous\n  if VirtualService changed → rebuild virtualServiceIndex else copy\n  if DestinationRule changed → rebuild destinationRuleIndex else copy\n  ... and so on for each config type\n```\n\nThis is critical for scaling: in a stable mesh with millions of services, a single ServiceEntry change doesn't rebuild the entire VirtualService index.\n\n### Service Translation\n\n#### Service Index Organization\n\nServices are indexed with visibility semantics:\n\n```\nServiceIndex:\n  privateByNamespace[ns] → services exportTo \".\" (same namespace only)\n  exportedToNamespace[ns] → services explicitly exported to this ns\n  public[] → services exportTo \"*\" (visible to all)\n  HostnameAndNamespace[hostname][ns] → specific service lookup\n```\n\nThis enables efficient filtering: when generating config for a sidecar in `ns-a`, the generator quickly finds all visible services without scanning the entire mesh.\n\n#### VirtualService Translation\n\nVirtualServices are indexed per gateway and namespace:\n\n```\nVirtualServiceIndex:\n  publicByGateway[gw] → VS exportTo \"*\" for this gateway\n  privateByNamespaceAndGateway[ns/name][gw] → VS in same namespace\n  exportedToNamespaceByGateway[ns/name][gw] → explicitly exported VS\n  delegates[vs] → delegate VS chains for hierarchical routing\n```\n\n**Route Generation**: When the RdsGenerator builds routes for a sidecar in `ns-a` targeting destination `svc.ns-b`, it:\n1. Looks up `svc.ns-b` service in ServiceIndex\n2. Finds VirtualServices matching `svc.ns-b` hostname visible to `ns-a`\n3. Extracts http/tcp routes from matching VirtualServices\n4. Applies DestinationRules (subset selection, load balancing policies)\n5. Generates Envoy RouteConfiguration with retry policies, timeouts, etc.\n\n#### DestinationRule Consolidation\n\nMultiple DestinationRules for the same service are consolidated:\n\n```\nconsolidatedDestRules:\n  specificDestRules[hostname] → non-wildcard rules for this service\n  wildcardDestRules[hostname] → wildcard rules (apply to all services in domain)\n  exportTo tracking → which namespaces each rule applies to\n```\n\nWhen a generator builds a Cluster for `svc.ns-a`, it:\n1. Finds all applicable DestinationRules (namespace-local, exported, root namespace)\n2. Merges subset definitions\n3. Applies load balancing and outlier detection settings\n4. Configures mTLS policies per subset\n\n### Error Tracking and Metrics\n\n```go\nProxyStatus: map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n  [errorCode][proxyID] = ProxyPushStatus{\n      Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints,  // Resource generation status\n      TimeCreated,                              // When status was created\n  }\n```\n\nGenerators record errors here; they are exposed in debug endpoints and metrics.\n\n---\n\n## Component 4: Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Files**: `pilot/pkg/model/context.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/service.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\n### Service Discovery Integration\n\n#### ServiceDiscovery Interface\n\nImplemented by platform-specific service registries (Kubernetes, Consul, etc.):\n\n```go\ninterface ServiceDiscovery {\n    Services() []*Service\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n    InstancesByPort(service *Service, port int) []*ServiceInstance\n    GetProxyServiceInstances(proxy *Proxy) []*ServiceInstance\n    AppendServiceHandler(handler ServiceHandler)\n}\n```\n\n#### Kubernetes Controller\n\nThe Kubernetes implementation watches:\n- **Services and Endpoints**: K8s Service resources → Istio Service with instances\n- **Pods**: Workload metadata (labels, IPs)\n- **ServiceEntry resources**: Custom Istio ServiceEntry CRDs\n\nWhen changes occur:\n1. Converts K8s API objects to Istio's `Service` and `IstioEndpoint` models\n2. Calls `DiscoveryServer.SvcUpdate()` for service definition changes\n3. Calls `DiscoveryServer.EDSUpdate()` for endpoint/instance changes\n\n### The XDSUpdater Interface\n\nService registries call these methods on DiscoveryServer to signal changes:\n\n```go\ninterface XDSUpdater {\n    EDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, endpoints []*IstioEndpoint)\n    EDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, endpoints []*IstioEndpoint)\n    SvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, event Event)\n    ConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n}\n```\n\n**EDSUpdate vs. EDSCacheUpdate**:\n- `EDSUpdate`: Updates cache AND triggers push to proxies\n- `EDSCacheUpdate`: Updates cache only (for health-check-driven endpoint changes that don't need full propagation)\n\n### Aggregate Registry Pattern\n\nPilot supports multiple service registries (multiple Kubernetes clusters, Consul, ServiceEntry):\n\n```\nEnvironment:\n  ServiceDiscovery (interface)\n      ↓\n  AggregateController (multiple registries)\n      ├── Kubernetes Cluster 1 (local)\n      ├── Kubernetes Cluster 2 (remote)\n      ├── Consul\n      └── ServiceEntry (in-cluster only)\n```\n\nEach registry:\n- Runs independently, watching its own data source\n- Registers handlers with AggregateController\n- Calls XDSUpdater methods when state changes\n\nAggregateController:\n- Merges service lists from all registries\n- De-duplicates services (by hostname and namespace)\n- Collects endpoints from all registries for each service\n- Ensures consistent service identity across clusters\n\n### Multi-Cluster Support\n\n#### Service Aggregation\n\nWhen the mesh spans multiple clusters:\n\n```\nCluster A (local istiod):\n  ├── K8s Service \"svc.default\"  → endpoints from cluster A\n  │\nCluster B (remote istiod):\n  └── K8s Service \"svc.default\"  → endpoints from cluster B\n\nAggregateController on Cluster A:\n  Fetches remote cluster's services via Cluster B's Pilot\n  Merges: Service \"svc.default\" now has endpoints from BOTH clusters\n```\n\nMechanics:\n1. Remote cluster's Pilot publishes service and endpoint information\n2. Local istiod reads via gRPC (or service-to-service API)\n3. RemoteRegistry adapter in AggregateController consumes the feed\n4. Service definitions are unified; endpoints are aggregated\n\n#### Network Topology\n\nThe `MeshNetworks` configuration describes how clusters are reachable:\n\n```\nMeshNetworks:\n  network \"cluster-a\":\n    endpoints:\n      - ip: 10.0.0.0/16   (cluster A pods)\n    gateways:\n      - ip: 203.0.113.1    (ingress gateway for cross-network traffic)\n      - port: 15443\n\n  network \"cluster-b\":\n    endpoints:\n      - ip: 10.1.0.0/16    (cluster B pods)\n    gateways:\n      - ip: 203.0.113.2\n      - port: 15443\n```\n\nWhen generating routes for a sidecar in cluster A to reach a service in cluster B:\n1. The sidecar's proxy sees the service has endpoints in network \"cluster-b\"\n2. Routes direct traffic to the cluster-b gateway IP\n3. The gateway performs further routing to actual endpoints\n4. Mutual TLS ensures end-to-end encryption\n\n#### Endpoint Sharding\n\nThe `EndpointIndex` organizes endpoints by service and shard (registry):\n\n```go\nEndpointIndex:\n  endpoints[service][shard] = []*IstioEndpoint\n\n  Example:\n  endpoints[\"svc.ns\"][kubernetes/cluster-1] = [pod-1, pod-2]\n  endpoints[\"svc.ns\"][kubernetes/cluster-2] = [pod-3, pod-4]\n```\n\nWhen EdsGenerator builds an EDS response:\n1. Collects endpoints from all shards\n2. Applies network locality filters\n3. Removes unhealthy endpoints (if health checking enabled)\n4. Groups by network/zone for locality-aware load balancing\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Config Change to Proxy Update\n\n### Full Push Scenario\n\n```\nScenario: User updates a VirtualService in namespace \"default\"\n\n1. ConfigStore (etcd watcher) detects VirtualService change\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate(PushRequest{\n       ConfigsUpdated: {kind.VirtualService, \"default\", \"my-vs\"}\n       Full: true\n       Reason: \"VirtualServiceUpdate\"\n   })\n\n2. ConfigUpdate() sends to pushChannel\n   └─> handleUpdates() debouncer waits for quiet period (default 100ms)\n   └─> Merges other updates arriving during quiet period\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.Push()\n\n3. Push() initializes new PushContext\n   └─> PushContext.InitContext() called\n   └─> updateContext() detects VirtualService change\n   └─> Rebuilds virtualServiceIndex (reuses others)\n   └─> Records PushVersion: \"v12345\"\n\n4. Push() calls AdsPushAll(req)\n   └─> Iterates adsClients map\n   └─> For each proxy:\n     └─> Checks if affected (ProxyNeedsPush)\n     └─> Enqueues Event to proxy's pushQueue with req.Push = PushContext\n\n5. sendPushes() goroutine processes pushQueue\n   └─> For each queued proxy:\n     └─> Acquires concurrentPushLimit slot\n     └─> Calls pushConnection(proxy, event)\n         └─> For each resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS):\n           └─> Gets appropriate generator\n           └─> Calls Generator.Generate(proxy, req.Push, watchedResource)\n           └─> Lookup cache for digest\n           └─> If changed: wrap in DiscoveryResponse, send via gRPC\n     └─> Releases slot\n\n6. Proxy receives DiscoveryResponse\n   └─> Parses routes, applies to Envoy config\n   └─> Sends ACK with nonce\n   └─> Traffic now routes according to new VirtualService\n```\n\n### Incremental (EDS) Push Scenario\n\n```\nScenario: Pod scales up in Deployment backing service \"web\"\n\n1. Kubernetes controller detects new Pod\n   └─> IstioEndpoint created with pod IP/labels\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.EDSUpdate(\n       shard: \"kubernetes/local-cluster\"\n       serviceName: \"web\"\n       namespace: \"default\"\n       endpoints: [old-eps..., new-eps...]\n   )\n\n2. EDSUpdate() updates EndpointIndex\n   └─> EndpointIndex.UpdateServiceEndpoints()\n   └─> Returns pushType = IncrementalPush\n   └─> Calls ConfigUpdate(PushRequest{\n       Full: false,\n       ConfigsUpdated: {kind.ServiceEntry, \"web\", \"default\"}\n       Reason: \"EndpointUpdate\"\n   })\n\n3. handleUpdates() debouncer (EDS debouncing may be disabled)\n   └─> Calls Push() immediately OR waits (depending on enableEDSDebounce)\n\n4. Push() on incremental request\n   └─> Does NOT rebuild PushContext (req.Push reused)\n   └─> Calls AdsPushAll() with req.Push = old PushContext\n\n5. pushConnection() for each proxy\n   └─> Gets EdsGenerator\n   └─> Calls EdsGenerator.Generate() with same PushContext\n   └─> EdsGenerator consults updated EndpointIndex\n   └─> Generates new Cluster with all endpoints\n   └─> Cache hit/miss detection\n   └─> If endpoints changed, sends new EDS response\n\n6. Proxy receives EDS update\n   └─> Updates endpoint list in Cluster \"outbound|80||web.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   └─> Immediately load-balances traffic to new pod\n```\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Resource Generators\n\nImplement `model.XdsResourceGenerator` to customize config generation:\n\n```go\ntype CustomCdsGenerator struct {\n    ConfigGenerator core.ConfigGenerator\n}\n\nfunc (g *CustomCdsGenerator) Generate(\n    proxy *model.Proxy,\n    req *model.PushRequest,\n    watched *model.WatchedResource,\n) (model.Resources, model.XdsLogDetails, error) {\n    // Custom cluster generation logic\n    return resources, logDetails, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Usage**: Register in DiscoveryServer.Generators:\n```go\nds.Generators[\"custom/ClusterType\"] = &CustomCdsGenerator{}\n```\n\nProxies with metadata `Generator: \"custom\"` will use this generator.\n\n### 2. Custom Service Registries\n\nImplement `ServiceDiscovery` and register with Environment:\n\n```go\ntype CustomRegistry struct{}\n\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) Services() []*Service { ... }\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) GetService(h host.Name) *Service { ... }\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) AppendServiceHandler(h ServiceHandler) { ... }\n```\n\nThe registry's `AppendServiceHandler` calls are invoked when DiscoveryServer initializes.\n\n### 3. Proxy Filtering\n\nOverride `DiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush` to implement custom push filtering:\n\n```go\nds.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Skip push if proxy doesn't care about changed configs\n    if req.Full {\n        return req, true\n    }\n    // Filter ConfigsUpdated\n    ...\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Telemetry and Callbacks\n\nService registries can implement callbacks for push completion:\n\n```go\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n    ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest)\n}\n\n// Wrapping the updater with logging/metrics\ntype MetricsUpdater struct {\n    inner XDSUpdater\n}\n\nfunc (m *MetricsUpdater) ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    log.Infof(\"Config update: %v\", req.Reason)\n    m.inner.ConfigUpdate(req)\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Authentication and Authorization\n\nCustom authenticators can be provided:\n\n```go\ntype Authenticator interface {\n    Authenticate(ctx context.Context) ([]string, error)\n}\n\nds.Authenticators = append(ds.Authenticators, &CustomAuthenticator{})\n```\n\nThe Connection initialization uses these to verify proxy identity.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Push Failures\n\nIf a generator encounters an error:\n\n```go\nif err != nil {\n    // Record error in PushContext for debugging\n    ps.AddMetric(monitoring.ProxyPushError, proxyID, \"route generation failed\")\n    // Continue with other proxies\n    return nil, nil, err\n}\n```\n\nErrors are tracked per proxy in `PushContext.ProxyStatus` and exposed via:\n- Debug endpoints: `/debug/push_status`\n- Metrics: `pilot_push_errors{type=\"routes\"}`\n\n### Connection Failures\n\nIf a proxy disconnects:\n- `closeConnection()` removes it from adsClients\n- Handlers unregistered to stop receiving updates\n- Next push to that proxy will be skipped (not in adsClients)\n- When proxy reconnects, it receives full config\n\n### Service Registry Failures\n\nIf a registry becomes unavailable (Kubernetes API server down):\n- That registry's controller stops; handler calls cease\n- Existing endpoints remain in EndpointIndex\n- Pushes continue with stale but consistent view\n- When registry recovers, incremental updates catch up\n\n### Validation Errors\n\nInvalid Istio resources (e.g., VirtualService referencing non-existent service):\n- Detected during config parsing\n- Recorded in config status (typically handled by admission controller)\n- Generators skip invalid resources\n- Meshes remain operational with partial config\n\n---\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Immutable PushContext\n\nEach push gets a snapshot of configuration. This:\n- Prevents races where config changes during push\n- Enables deterministic resource generation\n- Simplifies incremental vs. full push logic\n- Allows easy metrics/debugging per push version\n\n### 2. Debouncing at Core\n\nRather than debouncing in each handler, central debouncer merges:\n- Config changes\n- Service endpoint changes\n- Custom events\n\nThis avoids duplicate work and provides unified metrics.\n\n### 3. Per-Proxy Event Queue\n\nEach proxy has its own queue (`pushQueue`), ensuring:\n- Ordering of updates to a single proxy\n- No head-of-line blocking (slow proxy doesn't block others)\n- Easy to track per-proxy push metrics\n\n### 4. Generator Interface\n\nSeparating generation (`Generator.Generate()`) from push delivery allows:\n- Pluggable generators per resource type\n- Caching across multiple proxies\n- Async generation (generators can be CPU-intensive)\n\n### 5. Service Visibility Semantics\n\nExplicit exportTo policy prevents:\n- Accidental service leakage across boundaries\n- Load on generators computing routes for unreachable services\n- Configuration explosion in multi-tenant meshes\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Scaling Bottlenecks and Mitigations\n\n| Bottleneck | Impact | Mitigation |\n|-----------|--------|-----------|\n| Large number of proxies | Push delivery slow | concurrentPushLimit semaphore, per-proxy queue |\n| Frequent config changes | Debouncer overrun | Debounce timing tuning, pushChannel buffer |\n| Large services (many endpoints) | EDS response size | Sharding, endpoint subsetting |\n| Complex VirtualServices | Route generation slow | Generator caching, RDS delta pushes |\n| Multi-cluster service aggregation | InitContext latency | Incremental updates, reuse of unchanged indices |\n\n### Caching Strategy\n\n- **XDS Cache**: Stores serialized Envoy resources; invalidated on config changes\n- **Index Cache**: Service and VirtualService indices built once per push; reused for all proxies\n- **Endpoint Cache**: EndpointIndex updated incrementally; full rebuild on shard change\n\n### Metrics for Monitoring\n\n- `pilot_push_duration_seconds`: Time to complete a full push\n- `pilot_push_errors`: Number of push failures per type\n- `pilot_proxy_queue_time`: Time a proxy waits in push queue\n- `pilot_debounce_time`: Time spent debouncing before push\n- `envoy_xds_latency`: End-to-end latency from change to proxy acknowledgment\n\n---\n\n## Source File Reference\n\nKey implementation files:\n\n| Component | File | Responsibility |\n|-----------|------|-----------------|\n| **DiscoveryServer** | `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` | Core gRPC server, push coordination, debouncing |\n| **ADS/Connection** | `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` | Stream lifecycle, per-proxy request handling |\n| **PushContext** | `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` | Configuration snapshot, service/route/policy indices |\n| **Service Model** | `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` | Service and endpoint abstractions |\n| **Environment** | `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` | Mesh-wide state, ServiceDiscovery coordination |\n| **Controller** | `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go` | Event handler registration, AggregateController |\n| **CDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` | Cluster resource generation |\n| **RDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` | Route resource generation |\n| **LDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` | Listener resource generation |\n| **EDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` | Endpoint resource generation |\n| **Push Queue** | `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` | Per-proxy push queue with merge semantics |\n| **xDS Generators** | `pilot/pkg/networking/core` | Low-level Envoy config builders (routing, clustering, filtering) |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nPilot's Discovery Service is a sophisticated system for bridging Istio's declarative service mesh configuration with Envoy's imperative proxy configuration model. It achieves scale through:\n- **Immutable snapshots** for deterministic, concurrent generation\n- **Efficient indexing** of services and configurations\n- **Aggressive debouncing** to handle bursty updates\n- **Incremental pushes** for endpoint changes\n- **Pluggable architecture** for custom generators and registries\n\nUnderstanding this architecture is essential for:\n- Debugging configuration delivery issues\n- Optimizing mesh performance for specific workloads\n- Extending Istio with custom routing policies or service integrations\n- Contributing to Pilot's core functionality\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3645,"cache_read_input_tokens":82634,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3645},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"da3fe3bf-fda0-4888-a52d-5a81d10c9d61","uuid":"407e9af2-eabe-4f29-896f-b281a1be6289"}

The Discovery Service translates high-level Istio resources (VirtualServices, DestinationRules, Gateways, etc.) into low-level Envoy-specific resource configurations (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints) and maintains real-time synchronization as the service mesh state evolves.\n\nThe architecture follows a **push-based model** where Pilot proactively delivers configuration updates to proxies rather than waiting for proxies to poll. It supports Envoy's xDS v3 protocol in both state-of-the-world (full) and incremental push modes, with sophisticated debouncing and rate-limiting to handle high-frequency updates efficiently in large-scale meshes.\n\n---\n\n## Component 1: DiscoveryServer — The xDS gRPC Server\n\n**File**: `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe `DiscoveryServer` is the central gRPC server component that:\n- Implements Envoy's xDS APIs (ADS, CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS, SDS)\n- Manages active proxy connections via the `adsClients` map\n- Coordinates configuration pushes with debouncing and rate limiting\n- Maintains the global configuration snapshot (PushContext)\n- Serves as the interface between Istio's configuration model and Envoy proxies\n\n### Structure\n\n```go\ntype DiscoveryServer struct {\n    Env *model.Environment                           // Pilot's data model\n    Generators map[string]model.XdsResourceGenerator  // Per-type resource generators\n    adsClients map[string]*Connection                // Active proxy connections\n    adsClientsMutex sync.RWMutex                     // Protects adsClients\n\n    pushChannel chan *model.PushRequest              // Debounce buffer\n    pushQueue *PushQueue                             // Queue before actual push\n\n    concurrentPushLimit chan struct{}                // Semaphore for concurrent pushes\n    RequestRateLimit *rate.Limiter                   // Throttle incoming requests\n\n    Cache model.XdsCache                             // XDS resource cache\n    DebounceOptions DebounceOptions                  // Debounce timing config\n}\n```\n\n### Key Methods\n\n#### 1. **StreamAggregatedResources / Stream()**\nImplements the gRPC service method that establishes a bidirectional stream with an Envoy proxy.\n\n```\nConnection Flow:\n  1. Proxy connects → gRPC calls Stream()\n  2. Stream() checks server readiness and applies rate limiting\n  3. Authenticates the connection (mutual TLS verification)\n  4. Creates a Connection wrapper for the stream\n  5. Hands off to xds.Stream() for managing the connection lifecycle\n```\n\nThe server waits for `CachesSynced()` before accepting connections, ensuring proxies don't receive incomplete configuration during startup.\n\n#### 2. **ConfigUpdate(req \\*PushRequest)**\nCalled by event handlers (config watchers, service registry updates) to request a configuration push.\n\n```\nFlow:\n  1. Receives push request with updated configs/services\n  2. Sends to pushChannel for debouncing\n  3. handleUpdates() debouncer merges multiple rapid requests\n  4. Eventually calls Push() once config settles\n```\n\n#### 3. **Push(req \\*PushRequest)**\nExecutes the actual push once debouncing is complete.\n\n```\nFor Full Pushes:\n  1. Creates new PushContext by calling initPushContext()\n    - Rebuilds service index from service registry\n    - Rebuilds VirtualService and DestinationRule indexes\n    - Recomputes sidecar scopes\n    - Initializes ambient index\n  2. Calls dropCacheForRequest() to clear cached xDS responses\n  3. Calls AdsPushAll(req) to broadcast to connected proxies\n\nFor Incremental Pushes:\n  1. Reuses existing PushContext\n  2. Only clears cache for updated configs\n  3. Calls AdsPushAll() for affected proxies\n```\n\n#### 4. **AdsPushAll(req \\*PushRequest)**\nBroadcasts a push to all connected proxies.\n\n```\nAlgorithm:\n  1. Iterates through adsClients map (protected by RWMutex)\n  2. For each proxy connection, determines if push is necessary:\n     - Uses ProxyNeedsPush callback to filter proxies\n     - Checks if proxy is affected by specific config changes\n  3. Enqueues push event into pushQueue for the proxy\n  4. Returns immediately; actual push happens asynchronously in sendPushes()\n```\n\n#### 5. **sendPushes(stopCh)**\nBackground goroutine that processes the push queue.\n\n```\nFlow:\n  1. Dequeues a proxy from pushQueue\n  2. Acquires a slot from concurrentPushLimit semaphore\n  3. Calls pushConnection() to compute and send config for the proxy\n  4. Releases semaphore slot\n  5. Marks proxy as done in queue\n  6. Repeats until stopCh signals shutdown\n```\n\n### Cache Management\n\nThe DiscoveryServer maintains a typed XDS resource cache (`Cache`) that stores computed Envoy resources (Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints). This cache:\n- Avoids recomputing identical resources for multiple proxies\n- Is cleared on full pushes or when specific config types change\n- Is optimized for incremental pushes where only affected resources are regenerated\n- Supports different cache backends (enabled/disabled via features)\n\n### Concurrency Control\n\n**Debouncing**: Rapid configuration changes are merged before generating Envoy resources:\n- `DebounceAfter`: Minimum quiet time to wait after last event\n- `debounceMax`: Maximum time to wait regardless of event frequency\n- Prevents configuration churn from flooding proxies\n\n**Rate Limiting**:\n- `RequestRateLimit`: Throttles new incoming XDS requests from clients\n- `concurrentPushLimit`: Limits concurrent xDS resource generation to prevent resource exhaustion\n\n---\n\n## Component 2: ADS and the Connection Model\n\n**Files**: `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go`, `pilot/pkg/xds/ads_test.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\nThe ADS (Aggregated Discovery Service) stream handler manages the life cycle of individual proxy connections, processes discovery requests, and coordinates push delivery to single proxies.\n\n### Connection Type\n\n```go\ntype Connection struct {\n    xds.Connection                          // Wraps gRPC stream\n    node *core.Node                         // Envoy's metadata\n    proxy *model.Proxy                      // Istio's proxy representation\n    deltaStream DeltaDiscoveryStream        // For Delta xDS mode\n    s *DiscoveryServer                      // Parent server reference\n    ids []string                            // Authenticated identities\n}\n```\n\nThe `Connection` acts as a bridge between Envoy's gRPC stream and Istio's internal proxy model, translating between the two representations.\n\n### Connection Lifecycle\n\n#### 1. **Stream Establishment**\n```\nStream() → initConnection() → newConnection() → xds.Stream()\n\nProcess:\n  1. Stream() receives gRPC connection from Envoy\n  2. Checks server readiness\n  3. Applies rate limiting to prevent thundering herd\n  4. Authenticates connection (validates mTLS identity)\n  5. Initializes PushContext if not already done\n  6. Creates Connection wrapper\n  7. Hands to xds.Stream() which manages the actual message exchange\n```\n\n#### 2. **initConnection()**\nInitializes proxy metadata when receiving the first discovery request.\n\n```go\nExecution:\n  1. Parses Envoy's node metadata (pod name, namespace, IP, etc.)\n  2. Creates Proxy object from node metadata\n  3. Applies cluster alias mapping (multi-cluster translation)\n  4. Adds connection to adsClients map with a unique ID\n  5. Sets proxy's LastPushContext for monotonic push ordering\n  6. Registers handlers for this proxy with service registry\n```\n\n#### 3. **Request Processing: processRequest()**\nHandles individual discovery requests from the proxy.\n\n```go\nProcess:\n  1. Extracts resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS)\n  2. Checks if proxy should respond based on nonce/version\n  3. Creates PushRequest with:\n     - Full=true for missing resources or debug requests\n     - Delta for resource subscription changes\n     - Forced=true to bypass recent push filters\n  4. Calls pushXds() to generate and send response\n```\n\n**Key Insight**: `processRequest()` treats a discovery request as a push trigger, allowing proxies to explicitly request resources they're interested in.\n\n#### 4. **Push Delivery: pushConnection()**\nComputes and sends configuration for a single proxy.\n\n```go\nAlgorithm (per WatchedResource type):\n  1. Looks up the appropriate generator:\n     - CdsGenerator for Clusters\n     - RdsGenerator for Routes\n     - LdsGenerator for Listeners\n     - EdsGenerator for Endpoints\n  2. Calls generator.Generate(proxy, req) to build Envoy resources\n  3. Compares new resources with cached version\n  4. Sends only resources that changed (for incremental pushes)\n  5. Wraps in DiscoveryResponse with nonce and version info\n  6. Sends via gRPC stream to proxy\n```\n\nThe generator selection is proxy-aware; different proxies can use different generators (e.g., sidecar vs. gateway).\n\n#### 5. **Connection Cleanup: closeConnection()**\nRemoves proxy from active connection map when stream closes.\n\n```\nExecution:\n  1. Removes connection from adsClients\n  2. Removes proxy from service registry watchers\n  3. Unregisters proxy-specific handlers\n```\n\n### Push Coordination Through Events\n\nPushes are delivered via the `Event` structure:\n\n```go\ntype Event struct {\n    pushRequest *model.PushRequest\n    done func()                  // Must be called to signal completion\n}\n```\n\nThe `done()` callback ensures backpressure: the push queue won't dequeue the next proxy until `done()` is called, preventing the system from being overwhelmed.\n\n---\n\n## Component 3: PushContext — Configuration Snapshot and Translation\n\n**File**: `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go`\n\n### Responsibilities\n\n`PushContext` is an immutable snapshot of mesh configuration built once per full push. It:\n- Holds pre-computed indices of services, routes, policies, and security configurations\n- Serves as the authoritative configuration source for resource generators\n- Tracks push metrics and errors per proxy\n- Enables deterministic config translation across the fleet\n\n### Structure\n\n```go\ntype PushContext struct {\n    // Service catalog\n    ServiceIndex serviceIndex                        // Services indexed by namespace/visibility\n    virtualServiceIndex virtualServiceIndex          // VirtualServices by gateway\n    destinationRuleIndex destinationRuleIndex        // DestinationRules consolidated\n\n    // Security and networking\n    AuthnPolicies *AuthenticationPolicies            // RequestAuthentication, PeerAuthentication\n    AuthzPolicies *AuthorizationPolicies             // AuthorizationPolicy resources\n\n    // Configuration metadata\n    sidecarIndex sidecarIndex                        // Sidecar scopes per namespace\n    gatewayIndex gatewayIndex                        // Gateways by namespace\n\n    // Computed state\n    exportToDefaults exportToDefaults                // Default visibility rules\n    clusterLocalHosts ClusterLocalHosts              // Cluster-local service names\n\n    // Tracking\n    ProxyStatus map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus  // Push errors per proxy\n    PushVersion string                               // Unique push identifier\n}\n```\n\n### Initialization: InitContext()\n\nCalled once per full push to rebuild configuration.\n\n```\nExecution (createNewContext):\n  1. initServiceRegistry()\n    - Fetches all services from ServiceDiscovery (Kubernetes + ServiceEntry)\n    - Builds serviceIndex with private/public/exported-to organization\n    - Aggregates endpoints across multiple registries/clusters\n\n  2. initVirtualServices()\n    - Fetches all VirtualService resources\n    - Indexes by namespace, gateway, and delegation\n    - Validates references to services and subsets\n\n  3. initDestinationRules()\n    - Fetches all DestinationRule resources\n    - Consolidates rules for the same service across namespaces\n    - Pre-computes subset information\n\n  4. initAuthnPolicies() / initAuthorizationPolicies()\n    - Fetches authentication and authorization policies\n    - Builds efficient lookup structures by namespace/service\n\n  5. initSidecarScopes() [last, as it depends on all above]\n    - Computes SidecarScope for each namespace\n    - Default SidecarScope if none defined\n    - Determines ingress/egress visibility for workloads\n\n  6. initGateways() / initAmbient() / initWasmPlugins() / etc.\n    - Pre-computed data for gateways, ambient mesh, WASM plugins\n```\n\n**Incremental Updates**: If a previous PushContext exists and only specific config types changed, `updateContext()` reuses unchanged indices:\n\n```\nLogic:\n  if ServiceEntry changed → rebuild ServiceIndex else copy from previous\n  if VirtualService changed → rebuild virtualServiceIndex else copy\n  if DestinationRule changed → rebuild destinationRuleIndex else copy\n  ... and so on for each config type\n```\n\nThis is critical for scaling: in a stable mesh with millions of services, a single ServiceEntry change doesn't rebuild the entire VirtualService index.\n\n### Service Translation\n\n#### Service Index Organization\n\nServices are indexed with visibility semantics:\n\n```\nServiceIndex:\n  privateByNamespace[ns] → services exportTo \".\" (same namespace only)\n  exportedToNamespace[ns] → services explicitly exported to this ns\n  public[] → services exportTo \"*\" (visible to all)\n  HostnameAndNamespace[hostname][ns] → specific service lookup\n```\n\nThis enables efficient filtering: when generating config for a sidecar in `ns-a`, the generator quickly finds all visible services without scanning the entire mesh.\n\n#### VirtualService Translation\n\nVirtualServices are indexed per gateway and namespace:\n\n```\nVirtualServiceIndex:\n  publicByGateway[gw] → VS exportTo \"*\" for this gateway\n  privateByNamespaceAndGateway[ns/name][gw] → VS in same namespace\n  exportedToNamespaceByGateway[ns/name][gw] → explicitly exported VS\n  delegates[vs] → delegate VS chains for hierarchical routing\n```\n\n**Route Generation**: When the RdsGenerator builds routes for a sidecar in `ns-a` targeting destination `svc.ns-b`, it:\n1. Looks up `svc.ns-b` service in ServiceIndex\n2. Finds VirtualServices matching `svc.ns-b` hostname visible to `ns-a`\n3. Extracts http/tcp routes from matching VirtualServices\n4. Applies DestinationRules (subset selection, load balancing policies)\n5. Generates Envoy RouteConfiguration with retry policies, timeouts, etc.\n\n#### DestinationRule Consolidation\n\nMultiple DestinationRules for the same service are consolidated:\n\n```\nconsolidatedDestRules:\n  specificDestRules[hostname] → non-wildcard rules for this service\n  wildcardDestRules[hostname] → wildcard rules (apply to all services in domain)\n  exportTo tracking → which namespaces each rule applies to\n```\n\nWhen a generator builds a Cluster for `svc.ns-a`, it:\n1. Finds all applicable DestinationRules (namespace-local, exported, root namespace)\n2. Merges subset definitions\n3. Applies load balancing and outlier detection settings\n4. Configures mTLS policies per subset\n\n### Error Tracking and Metrics\n\n```go\nProxyStatus: map[string]map[string]ProxyPushStatus\n  [errorCode][proxyID] = ProxyPushStatus{\n      Clusters, Routes, Listeners, Endpoints,  // Resource generation status\n      TimeCreated,                              // When status was created\n  }\n```\n\nGenerators record errors here; they are exposed in debug endpoints and metrics.\n\n---\n\n## Component 4: Service Registry and Multi-Cluster Support\n\n**Files**: `pilot/pkg/model/context.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/service.go`, `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go`\n\n### Service Discovery Integration\n\n#### ServiceDiscovery Interface\n\nImplemented by platform-specific service registries (Kubernetes, Consul, etc.):\n\n```go\ninterface ServiceDiscovery {\n    Services() []*Service\n    GetService(hostname host.Name) *Service\n    InstancesByPort(service *Service, port int) []*ServiceInstance\n    GetProxyServiceInstances(proxy *Proxy) []*ServiceInstance\n    AppendServiceHandler(handler ServiceHandler)\n}\n```\n\n#### Kubernetes Controller\n\nThe Kubernetes implementation watches:\n- **Services and Endpoints**: K8s Service resources → Istio Service with instances\n- **Pods**: Workload metadata (labels, IPs)\n- **ServiceEntry resources**: Custom Istio ServiceEntry CRDs\n\nWhen changes occur:\n1. Converts K8s API objects to Istio's `Service` and `IstioEndpoint` models\n2. Calls `DiscoveryServer.SvcUpdate()` for service definition changes\n3. Calls `DiscoveryServer.EDSUpdate()` for endpoint/instance changes\n\n### The XDSUpdater Interface\n\nService registries call these methods on DiscoveryServer to signal changes:\n\n```go\ninterface XDSUpdater {\n    EDSUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, endpoints []*IstioEndpoint)\n    EDSCacheUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, endpoints []*IstioEndpoint)\n    SvcUpdate(shard ShardKey, hostname string, ns string, event Event)\n    ConfigUpdate(req *PushRequest)\n}\n```\n\n**EDSUpdate vs. EDSCacheUpdate**:\n- `EDSUpdate`: Updates cache AND triggers push to proxies\n- `EDSCacheUpdate`: Updates cache only (for health-check-driven endpoint changes that don't need full propagation)\n\n### Aggregate Registry Pattern\n\nPilot supports multiple service registries (multiple Kubernetes clusters, Consul, ServiceEntry):\n\n```\nEnvironment:\n  ServiceDiscovery (interface)\n      ↓\n  AggregateController (multiple registries)\n      ├── Kubernetes Cluster 1 (local)\n      ├── Kubernetes Cluster 2 (remote)\n      ├── Consul\n      └── ServiceEntry (in-cluster only)\n```\n\nEach registry:\n- Runs independently, watching its own data source\n- Registers handlers with AggregateController\n- Calls XDSUpdater methods when state changes\n\nAggregateController:\n- Merges service lists from all registries\n- De-duplicates services (by hostname and namespace)\n- Collects endpoints from all registries for each service\n- Ensures consistent service identity across clusters\n\n### Multi-Cluster Support\n\n#### Service Aggregation\n\nWhen the mesh spans multiple clusters:\n\n```\nCluster A (local istiod):\n  ├── K8s Service \"svc.default\"  → endpoints from cluster A\n  │\nCluster B (remote istiod):\n  └── K8s Service \"svc.default\"  → endpoints from cluster B\n\nAggregateController on Cluster A:\n  Fetches remote cluster's services via Cluster B's Pilot\n  Merges: Service \"svc.default\" now has endpoints from BOTH clusters\n```\n\nMechanics:\n1. Remote cluster's Pilot publishes service and endpoint information\n2. Local istiod reads via gRPC (or service-to-service API)\n3. RemoteRegistry adapter in AggregateController consumes the feed\n4. Service definitions are unified; endpoints are aggregated\n\n#### Network Topology\n\nThe `MeshNetworks` configuration describes how clusters are reachable:\n\n```\nMeshNetworks:\n  network \"cluster-a\":\n    endpoints:\n      - ip: 10.0.0.0/16   (cluster A pods)\n    gateways:\n      - ip: 203.0.113.1    (ingress gateway for cross-network traffic)\n      - port: 15443\n\n  network \"cluster-b\":\n    endpoints:\n      - ip: 10.1.0.0/16    (cluster B pods)\n    gateways:\n      - ip: 203.0.113.2\n      - port: 15443\n```\n\nWhen generating routes for a sidecar in cluster A to reach a service in cluster B:\n1. The sidecar's proxy sees the service has endpoints in network \"cluster-b\"\n2. Routes direct traffic to the cluster-b gateway IP\n3. The gateway performs further routing to actual endpoints\n4. Mutual TLS ensures end-to-end encryption\n\n#### Endpoint Sharding\n\nThe `EndpointIndex` organizes endpoints by service and shard (registry):\n\n```go\nEndpointIndex:\n  endpoints[service][shard] = []*IstioEndpoint\n\n  Example:\n  endpoints[\"svc.ns\"][kubernetes/cluster-1] = [pod-1, pod-2]\n  endpoints[\"svc.ns\"][kubernetes/cluster-2] = [pod-3, pod-4]\n```\n\nWhen EdsGenerator builds an EDS response:\n1. Collects endpoints from all shards\n2. Applies network locality filters\n3. Removes unhealthy endpoints (if health checking enabled)\n4. Groups by network/zone for locality-aware load balancing\n\n---\n\n## Data Flow: Config Change to Proxy Update\n\n### Full Push Scenario\n\n```\nScenario: User updates a VirtualService in namespace \"default\"\n\n1. ConfigStore (etcd watcher) detects VirtualService change\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.ConfigUpdate(PushRequest{\n       ConfigsUpdated: {kind.VirtualService, \"default\", \"my-vs\"}\n       Full: true\n       Reason: \"VirtualServiceUpdate\"\n   })\n\n2. ConfigUpdate() sends to pushChannel\n   └─> handleUpdates() debouncer waits for quiet period (default 100ms)\n   └─> Merges other updates arriving during quiet period\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.Push()\n\n3. Push() initializes new PushContext\n   └─> PushContext.InitContext() called\n   └─> updateContext() detects VirtualService change\n   └─> Rebuilds virtualServiceIndex (reuses others)\n   └─> Records PushVersion: \"v12345\"\n\n4. Push() calls AdsPushAll(req)\n   └─> Iterates adsClients map\n   └─> For each proxy:\n     └─> Checks if affected (ProxyNeedsPush)\n     └─> Enqueues Event to proxy's pushQueue with req.Push = PushContext\n\n5. sendPushes() goroutine processes pushQueue\n   └─> For each queued proxy:\n     └─> Acquires concurrentPushLimit slot\n     └─> Calls pushConnection(proxy, event)\n         └─> For each resource type (CDS, LDS, RDS, EDS):\n           └─> Gets appropriate generator\n           └─> Calls Generator.Generate(proxy, req.Push, watchedResource)\n           └─> Lookup cache for digest\n           └─> If changed: wrap in DiscoveryResponse, send via gRPC\n     └─> Releases slot\n\n6. Proxy receives DiscoveryResponse\n   └─> Parses routes, applies to Envoy config\n   └─> Sends ACK with nonce\n   └─> Traffic now routes according to new VirtualService\n```\n\n### Incremental (EDS) Push Scenario\n\n```\nScenario: Pod scales up in Deployment backing service \"web\"\n\n1. Kubernetes controller detects new Pod\n   └─> IstioEndpoint created with pod IP/labels\n   └─> Calls DiscoveryServer.EDSUpdate(\n       shard: \"kubernetes/local-cluster\"\n       serviceName: \"web\"\n       namespace: \"default\"\n       endpoints: [old-eps..., new-eps...]\n   )\n\n2. EDSUpdate() updates EndpointIndex\n   └─> EndpointIndex.UpdateServiceEndpoints()\n   └─> Returns pushType = IncrementalPush\n   └─> Calls ConfigUpdate(PushRequest{\n       Full: false,\n       ConfigsUpdated: {kind.ServiceEntry, \"web\", \"default\"}\n       Reason: \"EndpointUpdate\"\n   })\n\n3. handleUpdates() debouncer (EDS debouncing may be disabled)\n   └─> Calls Push() immediately OR waits (depending on enableEDSDebounce)\n\n4. Push() on incremental request\n   └─> Does NOT rebuild PushContext (req.Push reused)\n   └─> Calls AdsPushAll() with req.Push = old PushContext\n\n5. pushConnection() for each proxy\n   └─> Gets EdsGenerator\n   └─> Calls EdsGenerator.Generate() with same PushContext\n   └─> EdsGenerator consults updated EndpointIndex\n   └─> Generates new Cluster with all endpoints\n   └─> Cache hit/miss detection\n   └─> If endpoints changed, sends new EDS response\n\n6. Proxy receives EDS update\n   └─> Updates endpoint list in Cluster \"outbound|80||web.default.svc.cluster.local\"\n   └─> Immediately load-balances traffic to new pod\n```\n\n---\n\n## Extension Points\n\n### 1. Custom Resource Generators\n\nImplement `model.XdsResourceGenerator` to customize config generation:\n\n```go\ntype CustomCdsGenerator struct {\n    ConfigGenerator core.ConfigGenerator\n}\n\nfunc (g *CustomCdsGenerator) Generate(\n    proxy *model.Proxy,\n    req *model.PushRequest,\n    watched *model.WatchedResource,\n) (model.Resources, model.XdsLogDetails, error) {\n    // Custom cluster generation logic\n    return resources, logDetails, nil\n}\n```\n\n**Usage**: Register in DiscoveryServer.Generators:\n```go\nds.Generators[\"custom/ClusterType\"] = &CustomCdsGenerator{}\n```\n\nProxies with metadata `Generator: \"custom\"` will use this generator.\n\n### 2. Custom Service Registries\n\nImplement `ServiceDiscovery` and register with Environment:\n\n```go\ntype CustomRegistry struct{}\n\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) Services() []*Service { ... }\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) GetService(h host.Name) *Service { ... }\nfunc (r *CustomRegistry) AppendServiceHandler(h ServiceHandler) { ... }\n```\n\nThe registry's `AppendServiceHandler` calls are invoked when DiscoveryServer initializes.\n\n### 3. Proxy Filtering\n\nOverride `DiscoveryServer.ProxyNeedsPush` to implement custom push filtering:\n\n```go\nds.ProxyNeedsPush = func(proxy *model.Proxy, req *model.PushRequest) (*model.PushRequest, bool) {\n    // Skip push if proxy doesn't care about changed configs\n    if req.Full {\n        return req, true\n    }\n    // Filter ConfigsUpdated\n    ...\n}\n```\n\n### 4. Telemetry and Callbacks\n\nService registries can implement callbacks for push completion:\n\n```go\ntype XDSUpdater interface {\n    ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest)\n}\n\n// Wrapping the updater with logging/metrics\ntype MetricsUpdater struct {\n    inner XDSUpdater\n}\n\nfunc (m *MetricsUpdater) ConfigUpdate(req *model.PushRequest) {\n    log.Infof(\"Config update: %v\", req.Reason)\n    m.inner.ConfigUpdate(req)\n}\n```\n\n### 5. Authentication and Authorization\n\nCustom authenticators can be provided:\n\n```go\ntype Authenticator interface {\n    Authenticate(ctx context.Context) ([]string, error)\n}\n\nds.Authenticators = append(ds.Authenticators, &CustomAuthenticator{})\n```\n\nThe Connection initialization uses these to verify proxy identity.\n\n---\n\n## Error Handling\n\n### Push Failures\n\nIf a generator encounters an error:\n\n```go\nif err != nil {\n    // Record error in PushContext for debugging\n    ps.AddMetric(monitoring.ProxyPushError, proxyID, \"route generation failed\")\n    // Continue with other proxies\n    return nil, nil, err\n}\n```\n\nErrors are tracked per proxy in `PushContext.ProxyStatus` and exposed via:\n- Debug endpoints: `/debug/push_status`\n- Metrics: `pilot_push_errors{type=\"routes\"}`\n\n### Connection Failures\n\nIf a proxy disconnects:\n- `closeConnection()` removes it from adsClients\n- Handlers unregistered to stop receiving updates\n- Next push to that proxy will be skipped (not in adsClients)\n- When proxy reconnects, it receives full config\n\n### Service Registry Failures\n\nIf a registry becomes unavailable (Kubernetes API server down):\n- That registry's controller stops; handler calls cease\n- Existing endpoints remain in EndpointIndex\n- Pushes continue with stale but consistent view\n- When registry recovers, incremental updates catch up\n\n### Validation Errors\n\nInvalid Istio resources (e.g., VirtualService referencing non-existent service):\n- Detected during config parsing\n- Recorded in config status (typically handled by admission controller)\n- Generators skip invalid resources\n- Meshes remain operational with partial config\n\n---\n\n## Key Design Decisions\n\n### 1. Immutable PushContext\n\nEach push gets a snapshot of configuration. This:\n- Prevents races where config changes during push\n- Enables deterministic resource generation\n- Simplifies incremental vs. full push logic\n- Allows easy metrics/debugging per push version\n\n### 2. Debouncing at Core\n\nRather than debouncing in each handler, central debouncer merges:\n- Config changes\n- Service endpoint changes\n- Custom events\n\nThis avoids duplicate work and provides unified metrics.\n\n### 3. Per-Proxy Event Queue\n\nEach proxy has its own queue (`pushQueue`), ensuring:\n- Ordering of updates to a single proxy\n- No head-of-line blocking (slow proxy doesn't block others)\n- Easy to track per-proxy push metrics\n\n### 4. Generator Interface\n\nSeparating generation (`Generator.Generate()`) from push delivery allows:\n- Pluggable generators per resource type\n- Caching across multiple proxies\n- Async generation (generators can be CPU-intensive)\n\n### 5. Service Visibility Semantics\n\nExplicit exportTo policy prevents:\n- Accidental service leakage across boundaries\n- Load on generators computing routes for unreachable services\n- Configuration explosion in multi-tenant meshes\n\n---\n\n## Performance Considerations\n\n### Scaling Bottlenecks and Mitigations\n\n| Bottleneck | Impact | Mitigation |\n|-----------|--------|-----------|\n| Large number of proxies | Push delivery slow | concurrentPushLimit semaphore, per-proxy queue |\n| Frequent config changes | Debouncer overrun | Debounce timing tuning, pushChannel buffer |\n| Large services (many endpoints) | EDS response size | Sharding, endpoint subsetting |\n| Complex VirtualServices | Route generation slow | Generator caching, RDS delta pushes |\n| Multi-cluster service aggregation | InitContext latency | Incremental updates, reuse of unchanged indices |\n\n### Caching Strategy\n\n- **XDS Cache**: Stores serialized Envoy resources; invalidated on config changes\n- **Index Cache**: Service and VirtualService indices built once per push; reused for all proxies\n- **Endpoint Cache**: EndpointIndex updated incrementally; full rebuild on shard change\n\n### Metrics for Monitoring\n\n- `pilot_push_duration_seconds`: Time to complete a full push\n- `pilot_push_errors`: Number of push failures per type\n- `pilot_proxy_queue_time`: Time a proxy waits in push queue\n- `pilot_debounce_time`: Time spent debouncing before push\n- `envoy_xds_latency`: End-to-end latency from change to proxy acknowledgment\n\n---\n\n## Source File Reference\n\nKey implementation files:\n\n| Component | File | Responsibility |\n|-----------|------|-----------------|\n| **DiscoveryServer** | `pilot/pkg/xds/discovery.go` | Core gRPC server, push coordination, debouncing |\n| **ADS/Connection** | `pilot/pkg/xds/ads.go` | Stream lifecycle, per-proxy request handling |\n| **PushContext** | `pilot/pkg/model/push_context.go` | Configuration snapshot, service/route/policy indices |\n| **Service Model** | `pilot/pkg/model/service.go` | Service and endpoint abstractions |\n| **Environment** | `pilot/pkg/model/context.go` | Mesh-wide state, ServiceDiscovery coordination |\n| **Controller** | `pilot/pkg/model/controller.go` | Event handler registration, AggregateController |\n| **CDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/cds.go` | Cluster resource generation |\n| **RDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/rds.go` | Route resource generation |\n| **LDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/lds.go` | Listener resource generation |\n| **EDS Generator** | `pilot/pkg/xds/eds.go` | Endpoint resource generation |\n| **Push Queue** | `pilot/pkg/xds/pushqueue.go` | Per-proxy push queue with merge semantics |\n| **xDS Generators** | `pilot/pkg/networking/core` | Low-level Envoy config builders (routing, clustering, filtering) |\n\n---\n\n## Conclusion\n\nPilot's Discovery Service is a sophisticated system for bridging Istio's declarative service mesh configuration with Envoy's imperative proxy configuration model. It achieves scale through:\n- **Immutable snapshots** for deterministic, concurrent generation\n- **Efficient indexing** of services and configurations\n- **Aggressive debouncing** to handle bursty updates\n- **Incremental pushes** for endpoint changes\n- **Pluggable architecture** for custom generators and registries\n\nUnderstanding this architecture is essential for:\n- Debugging configuration delivery issues\n- Optimizing mesh performance for specific workloads\n- Extending Istio with custom routing policies or service integrations\n- Contributing to Pilot's core functionality\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
